As a Filipino, it is always nice to see my country represented in popular media like movies and games, even better when it's done right. It gives us a sense of pride in the thought that we are acknowledged especially in the international community (or at least that's how I see it). I only hope that these instances will not be the only times where we show that we are proud of our identity, and I believe that we Filipinos have a long way to go in the road to truly embracing our nation and culture.  For the knowledge and convenience of any foreigner that may stumble into this comments section, here are the Filipino vocabulary used in the trailer.  "Hay, buhay..." - "Oh, life..."/ "Ugh, life..." (commonly a sigh of bliss, exasperation or disappointment, depending on the context.) "Kontrolado ko 'to!" - "I can control this!"/ "I can handle this!"/ "I got this!" (colloquial form of "Kontrolado ko ito!")  Mabuhay! (Long live!)

I think i understand how her dash and electrification may work (at 0:52).  So im assuming this is her E because the other two skills are just utils and not the so called "signature" ability, meaning that it can be recharged with kills (since she is probably a duelist). The way i think it works is that you click it, and you go in this electrified mode where you run faster and you can still shoot at the enemies. I'm assuming it will last for something like 3-4 seconds and you can interrupt the ability beforehand by simply crouching, making it so that you do a slide before the ability is over. So the entirety of the clip at 0:52 is done in one single motion, you cant just dash whenever you want or run fast whenever you want. It seems strong but i'm assuming players will need to capitalize on those 3-4 seconds of electrification to entry on a site and/or score some take downs. Perfect Filipino cultural representation by @riot @valorant -She says "hay buhay" (dear life) -She says "kontrolado ko 'to" (i can control this) -Her English is so Pinoy -Her dog is an Aspin -Pilipinas 5 framed in her bedroom which shows her love for basketball -The interior of her room showcases pop culture in the Philippines and love for the Island life -Her tattoos and piercings are inspired by Filipino mythos - the Pintados (Painted Warriors) -Her colors blue and gold are lifted from the colors of the Philippine flag (Blue for peace and Gold for the sun rays) -She loves music and karaoke and is definitely into fun runs and marathons -The song used in this video is by Filipino artist under 88rising Ylona Garcia -And, MAHAL ANG SINGIL SA KURYENTE SA PINAS (electricity in the Ph is expensive) ergo her character abilities 'PUTAH, ANG SAYA!

This is just an assumption.  Neon's personality is definitely a kind and caring girl. Just the fact that her pet is an Aspin and she chose to be under Sage's command proves this.  The Aspin means Asong Pinoy which translates to Philippine Dog(yes we're great at names) and they may be the most common breed to own in the Philippines, but they're also the most common breed of strays here. They're also mostly neglected by some of the people because they're a "local" breed and would rather own a dog with a more notable breed such as Huskies, Shibas, Shih Tzus and Pits just to name a few.
